[30;1m209 | [0m[35mSince DEAP uses the Python parser to compile the code represented by the trees,[0m
[30;1m210 | [0m[35mit inherits from its limitations. The most commonly encountered restriction is[0m
[30;1m211 | [0m[35mthe parsing stack limit. The Python interpreter parser stack limit is usually[0m
[30;1m212 | [0m[35mfixed between 92 and 99. This means that an expression can at most be composed[0m
